                          The box set Live from the Atlantic Studios was by the Australian band who recorded the song "Let's Get It Up". It included a remastered version of this live album. It was produced by Robert John "Mutt" Lange.
                          • The box set Live from the Atlantic Studios was produced by Robert John "Mutt" Lange.
                          • The Australian band that recorded the song "Let's Get It Up" released the box set Live from the Atlantic Studios.
                          • The box set Live from the Atlantic Studios includes a remastered version of a live album.
                          • The Australian band that recorded the song "Let's Get It Up" also released a live album, which was included in the box set Live from the Atlantic Studios.
                          • Robert John "Mutt" Lange produced the live album that was included in the box set Live from the Atlantic Studios.

                            • Hegang
                            22 September 1791 is the birth date of this German scientist. His laboratory burner design was later perfected by another scientist, forming the device of which the Teclu burner is a hotter-flamed variant. This other scientist was the laboratory assistant of Robert Bunsen.
                            • A German scientist was born on 22 September 1791.
                            • This German scientist designed a laboratory burner.
                            • Another scientist perfected the laboratory burner design of the German scientist.
                            • The Teclu burner is a hotter-flamed variant of the burner designed by the other scientist.
                            • The other scientist was a laboratory assistant of Robert Bunsen.

                                The Day After, a 1982 film that aired in 1983, was the seventh highest rated non-sports show and featured an American state highway. The De Soto High School in the American state in the northeast is located off this highway. The album "I Like to Rock" was recorded in the American state.
                                • 1. The 1982 film, The Day After, aired in 1983.
                                • 2. The Day After was the seventh highest rated non-sports show in its time.
                                • 3. The Day After features an American state highway.
                                • 4. De Soto High School is located in an American state in the northeast.
                                • 5. De Soto High School is situated off the American state highway featured in The Day After.
                                • 6. The album "I Like to Rock" was recorded in the same American state as De Soto High School.
